 isse postped or pre-ped yugers ko 3 pratishat atirikt tex dena hoga

 ' India Mortgage Guarantee Corporation (IMGC) on Thursday released the results of its first ever home hunt (home search) survey
 isamen kaha gaya he ki aaj kii taarikh main sirf 32 pratishat bharatiyon ke paas ghar he or home finance kaa bhavishya acha he
 The Home Hunt (home search) survey is an annual research survey, which deals with the perspective and trends of housing and housing finance in India
 anusandhan kaa makasad bharat main ghar kharidne waalon kii soch, aavashyaktaa or chintaa ke bare main anuthi jaankaree muhaiyaa karana he
 The survey is conducted in 14 cities (metro, mini metro and small cities) of the country in association with Canter IMRB
 imjisi home hunt 1
 1 Research takes data from both people who have bought a house and who plan to buy
 imjisi home hunt ke nattejey jari karte hue neshnal houseing bank ke emdi or siio shriram kalyanraman or india mortges guarantee corporation ke siio amitabh mehara maujuud the
 The main results of the IMGC Home Hunt reveal that only 32 percent of the people live in own-bought homes and 56 percent are not planning to buy homes in the near future
 is surveykshan main bhaag lene waalon ne jo pramukh mushkilen bataayin unamem byaaj kii oonchi dar (38 pratishat), bachat na hona or udhaar lene kii ichha na hona (38 pratishat), sampatti kii baari keemat (32 pratishat) or karj kii aparyaapt uplabdhta (32 pratishat) shaamil he
 This indicates that there is a serious need to provide money for the house early in life
 pehali baar ghar kharidne vaale shuruaati bhugtan ke liye mukhya rup se nijee bachat par nirbhar karte hai
 This also delays buying a house
 yuvaaon main takreeban aadhe (46 pratishat) abhibhavakon ke saath rahete hai
 Are renters and live in their own homes (31 percent)
 isse abhibhavakon par aarthik nirbharta kaa pataa chalata he
 For loan-taking youth, 'no loan history' and 'getting the required amount in debt' is a bigger problem than others
 surveykshan main pataa chalaa he ki zyaadaatar maamalon main kiraye par rahanaa or ghar ke shuruaati bhugtan ke liye nijee bachat par nirbhar karne se ghar kharidne main deree hoti he
 It is noteworthy that in case of renting houses, 37% is much higher in small towns as compared to 29 percent in metro cities
 mini metro shaharon main to yah or bhi kam 23 pratishat hi he
 The comments yah data is tathy ko rekhaankit karata he ki bhale hi yuva kam umr main kamaane lage hai or ve ghar ke liye karj kii kistein chukaane main sakasham hai phir bhi shuruaati bhugtan, down pement ke liye paryaapt bachat nahin kar pate hai
 This research also shows that people in India want to make the initial payment for the house from their savings and 62 to 65 percent people depend on it

 aap apane kaam par dhyaan nahin de paa rahi hai? to shaayad aap apane bwoyfriend ke pyaar main hai
 According to a study published in a journal called Motivation and Emotion, people who are in love are unable to focus properly and do not perform well in tasks that need to be cautious
 shodhakarta wain steenbergan ke mutabik, 'jab aap kisi nae-nae romantic relationships main hote hai to duusari chizon main focus karnaa mushkil ho jaataa he, kyonki aapkaa cognitive risource (dimagi prakriya jisamen focus, yaaddaasht, samasyaon kaa samdhaan dhundne kii kshamta or tarkshakti shaamil he
 Thinking about his love all the time
 'wain steenbergan ne leden uniwarsity or uniwarsity of marilland ke apane sahyogiyon ke saath milakar un 43 logon kaa adhyayan kiya jo pichley chah maheene se relationships main the
 The people involved in the study were given several types of tasks, one of which they had to make a list of non-essential information
 natijatan jo log zyada pyaar main the ve is task main kam safal rahe
 There was no difference between women and men in terms of performance
 pratibhaagiyon se prashnawali puri karne se pehle-pehle romantic mujeec sunate hue romantic date ke bare main bhi sochane ko kaha gaya tha
 Stein Bergen says, "it is not yet known why romantic love and cognitive control are interlinked
" 'unhone kaha, 'shaayad aisa ho saktaa he ki premi / premika apane cognitive risource kaa istemaal sirf apane pyaar ke bare main sochane ke liye karte hon or boring task ke liye unke paas koi risource hi nahin bachataa

 aisi hi kahani naveen patnayak kii he
 When the former Chief Minister of Odisha Biju Patnaik died on April 17, 1997, his son Naveen Patnaik had no distance from politics
 naveen patnayak (naveen Patnaik) america main rahete the
 He had no special relationship with Oriya language and culture and he could not speak Odia language properly
 biju patnayak kii maut ke baad party ko koun sanbhale, is baat lekar bahes shuru ho gai
 Biju Patnaik was an influential leader
 azaadi kii ladaai ke dauraan jail main bhi rahe the
 He has been the Chief Minister of Odisha twice, as well as MP and minister at the Center several times
 biju patnayak sabase pehle congress kii taraf se 1961 main do saal ke liye mukhyamantri kii kursi sanbhali
 Then in 1990, he was Chief Minister on behalf of the Janata Dal for a full five years
 pichley loksabhaa or vidhansabha chunaavon main bhi bijd ne shandaar pradarshan kiya tha
